# Text Elements
The rate of forward reaction is equal to the rate of backward
reaction, as well as the Concentration of both side is 
constant ^k0M5H1EJ

Reverse reaction is endothermic as Increase in temperature
favors the endothermic reaction ^5JYROOH5

The left hand side ^MbwQ3Xqt

Because the left hand side has more moles. and Inc
pressure means that it prefers the more mole side ^DyNyVvaG

The mixture becomes more dark brown color ^6pJciKXi

The rate of forward reaction is equal to backward reaction -(1)
Concentrations on both sides stay constant ^hn6UoIie

It increases ^umQlB9y1

An increase in pressure prefers the side with the less 
moles ^ynq4tLLd

Because both side have the same mole ^jJ6MWIma

The more pressure it has, It will prefer the less moles side
since reactant side has less moles, Position of eq
is there ^kMErq6A9

The backward direction is endothermic as increase in temperature is
creating more % of NO2, HENCE THE FORWARD reaction must be 
exothermic ^uGg3MM8z

Increase in pressure causes the position of equilibrium to go on the 
less moles side, Hence more N2O4 is made which is pale yellow. ^zIuDHnfL
